			flag = USA_Lend_Lease_to_FRA4

	offset = 15 # Check for trigger conditions every 15 days
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = june year = 1999 }

		name = ACTION_NAME_OK

event = {
	id = 2048840
	random = no
	country = SOV
	persistent = yes

	decision = { 
		exists = FRA
		NOT = { war = { country = FRA country = SOV } }
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA1 flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA2 flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA3 flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA4 }
				war = { country = FRA country = GER }
				war = { country = FRA country = ENG }
				NOT = { war = { country = FRA country = SOV } }
				NOT = {	lost_national = { country = SOV value = 5 } }
				OR = { 
					lost_national = { country = FRA value = 3 }
					control = { province = 116 data = -2 } #Brussels
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = { flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA1 flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA2 flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA3 flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA4 }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						war = { country = FRA country = GER }
						war = { country = FRA country = ENG }
						NOT = { war = { country = FRA country = SOV } }
						NOT = {	lost_national = { country = SOV value = 7 } }
						OR = { 
							lost_national = { country = FRA value = 1 }
							control = { province = 116 data = -2 } #Brussels
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = { NOT = { lost_national = { country = FRA value = 10 } } flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA3 }
			AND = { lost_national = { country = FRA value = 10 } flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA1 }
		}
	}

	name = "Lend-Lease program for France"
	desc = 3700desc
	style = 2
	picture = "lend_lease"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 15 # Check for trigger conditions every 15 days
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = june year = 1999 }

		trigger = {
			NOT = { flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA1 }
			#for human or AI. AI will pick this if France isn't facing a major invasion
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOT = { lost_national = { country = FRA value = 10 } }
			}
		}
		name = "Small"

event = {
	id = 2048841
	random = no
	country = FRA
	persistent = yes

	name = "End of the Lend-Lease for France"
	desc = "France will no longer receive Lend-Lease aid."
	style = 2
	picture = "lend_lease"
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA1
			flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA2
			flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA3
			flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA4
		}
		NOT = {	exists = SOV }
	}
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 15 # Check for trigger conditions every 15 days
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = june year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { type = clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA1 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA2 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA3 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_FRA4 }
		
		command = { type = trigger which = 2048842 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 2048881
	random = no
	country = ENG
	persistent = yes

	name = "End of the Lend-Lease for Britain"
	desc = "Britain will no longer receive Lend-Lease aid."
	style = 2
	picture = "lend_lease"
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			flag = JAP_Lend_Lease_to_ENG1
			flag = JAP_Lend_Lease_to_ENG2
			flag = JAP_Lend_Lease_to_ENG3
			flag = JAP_Lend_Lease_to_ENG4
		}
		NOT = {	exists = JAP }
	}
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 15 # Check for trigger conditions every 15 days
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = june year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { type = clrflag which = JAP_Lend_Lease_to_ENG1 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = JAP_Lend_Lease_to_ENG2 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = JAP_Lend_Lease_to_ENG3 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = JAP_Lend_Lease_to_ENG4 }
		
		command = { type = trigger which = 2048882 }
	}
}

	id = 2048931
	random = no
	country = INO
	persistent = yes

	name = "End of the Lend-Lease for Indonesia"
	desc = "Indonesia will no longer receive Lend-Lease aid."
	style = 2
	picture = "lend_lease"
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_INO1
			flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_INO2
			flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_INO3
			flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_INO4
		}
		NOT = {	exists = SOV }
	}
	
	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 15 # Check for trigger conditions every 15 days
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = june year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { type = clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_INO1 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_INO2 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_INO3 }
		command = { type = clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_INO4 }
		
		command = { type = trigger which = 2048932 }
	}
}

		command = { trigger = { local_flag = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_IRQ4_local } type = local_clrflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_IRQ4_local }

		command = { type = extra_tc value = 5 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SOV_Lend_Lease_to_IRQ1_local }
	}
